describes the active authentication architecture.\n\n## Active Flows\n\n- Password auth (username/email + password)\n- Google OAuth login\n- Google account linking/unlinking from an authenticated profile\n\nEmail verification code remains in the repository for future re-enable, but it is not part of the active flow.\n\n## Base Path\n\n`/api/v1/auth`\n\n## Endpoints\n\n### 1) `GET /csrf-token`\nReturns an anonymous CSRF token and sets `anon_csrf` cookie.\n\n### 2) `POST /register`\nCreates a user account (does not auto-login).\n\nRequest body:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"username\": \"pilotname\",\n  \"email\": \"player@example.com\",\n  \"password\": \"StrongPass123\"\n}\n```\n\nResponse:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"message\": \"User registered successfully\",\n  \"user\": {\n \"updated_at\": \"...\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 3) `POST /login`\nLogs in with `identifier` (username or email) + password.\nSets access/refresh JWT cookies and CSRF cookies.\n\n### 4) `GET /google/login`\nStarts Google OAuth login redirect flow.\n\n### 5) `GET /google/callback`\nHandles OAuth callback, creates or links account, issues JWT cookies, redirects to frontend.\n\n### 6) `POST /google/link/start`\nAuthenticated endpoint to begin linking a Google account to the current user.\n\n### 7) `POST /google/unlink`\nAuthenticated endpoint to unlink the currently linked Google account.\n\n### 8) `GET /me`\nReturns current authenticated user profile.\n\n### 9) `PATCH /me/username`\nUpdates the in-game username for the authenticated user.\n\n### 10) `POST /refresh`\nRefreshes access token using refresh token cookie + refresh CSRF token.\n\n### 11) `POST /logout`\nClears auth and CSRF cookies.\n\n## Environment Variables (Auth)\n\nRequired:\n- `SECRET_KEY`\n- `JWT_SECRET_KEY`\n\nGoogle OAuth:\n- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`\n- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`\n- `BACKEND_PUBLIC_BASE_URL`\n- `FRONTEND_PUBLIC_BASE_URL`\n- `GOOGLE_OAUTH_REDIRECT_PATH`\n- decodeURIComponent(match[1]) : ''\n}\n\nfunction assertSecureAuthTransport(): void {\n  const apiUrl = new URL(API_BASE_URL, window.location.origin)\n  const pageProtocol = window.location.protocol\n  const apiProtocol = apiUrl.protocol\n  const allowInsecure = import.meta.env.DEV && import.meta.env.VITE_ALLOW_INSECURE_AUTH === 'true'\n\n  if (isLocalhost(apiUrl.hostname) || allowInsecure) return\n  if (pageProtocol === 'https:' && apiProtocol === 'https:') return\n\n  throw new AuthApiError(\n    'Secure auth requires HTTPS for both frontend and backend. Set VITE_API_BASE_URL_DEV or VITE_API_BASE_URL_PROD to an https:// endpoint.',\n    0,\n    null,\n  )\n}\n\nasync function parseJsonSafe(response: Response): Promise<unknown> {\n  try {\n    return await response.json()\n  } catch {\n    return null\n  }\n}\n\nfunction formatValidationErrors(errors: ApiValidationError[] | undefined): string[] {\n  if (!errors || errors.length === 0) return []\n  return errors.map((error) => {\n    const path = Array.isArray(error.loc) ? error.loc.join('.') : 'field'\n    const message = error.msg ??
